<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Walkthrough">Walkthrough</span></h2>
<p>Talk to <a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a> to start the <a href="/wiki/Quest" title="Quest">quest</a> after entering <a href="/wiki/The_Cavern_of_Wrath" title="The Cavern of Wrath">The Cavern of Wrath</a> or after encountering <a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a>. The reward can be received as soon as the quest starts.
</p><p><br />
<b><a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a>:</b> <i><a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a> dwells in the caves beyond the wrecks, at the head of Siren's Cove.<br /><br />Leave her be and we can only hope that she continues to return the favour.  </i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kill_Merveil"><a href="/wiki/File:Quest_Notification.png" class="image"><img alt="Quest Notification.png" src="/w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/30px-Quest_Notification.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="30" height="29" srcset="/w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/45px-Quest_Notification.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/60px-Quest_Notification.png 2x" data-file-width="86" data-file-height="83" /></a> Kill <a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a></span></h3>
<p>Kill <a href="/wiki/Merveil,_the_Siren" title="Merveil, the Siren">Merveil, the Siren</a>, in her lair. You can also talk to <a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a> in town for help with the battle.
</p><p><br />
If you haven't encountered <a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a> you can claim the quest reward now to assist you with the battle.
</p><p><b><a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a>:</b> <i>If you must take your chances with the Siren, then have this. It may be of some help.<br /><br />But please, know that you don't have to do this. <a href="/wiki/Tarkleigh" title="Tarkleigh">Tarkleigh</a> and I are getting used to having you around.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enter_the_Forest"><a href="/wiki/File:Quest_Notification.png" class="image"><img alt="Quest Notification.png" src="/w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/30px-Quest_Notification.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="30" height="29" srcset="/w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/45px-Quest_Notification.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/60px-Quest_Notification.png 2x" data-file-width="86" data-file-height="83" /></a> Enter the Forest</span></h3>
<p>You have killed <a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a>. Find the exit in her lair to enter the forest.
</p><p><br />
<b><a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a>:</b> <i>First I thought you brave, then a fool for seeking out <a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a>. A fool in love with death. Now... I don't know.<br /><br />The coast is ours, thanks to you. But please, keep one thing in mind for me. What have you become when even nightmares fear you?</i>
</p><p><b><a href="/wiki/Tarkleigh" title="Tarkleigh">Tarkleigh</a>:</b> <i>Damn me! I didn't think it possible. All those souls <a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a> and her brood have consumed over the years... you've done right by those that are dead, and by those who still might live.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quest_Complete"><a href="/wiki/File:Quest_Notification.png" class="image"><img alt="Quest Notification.png" src="/w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/30px-Quest_Notification.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="30" height="29" srcset="/w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/45px-Quest_Notification.png 1.5x, /w/images/thumb/5/57/Quest_Notification.png/60px-Quest_Notification.png 2x" data-file-width="86" data-file-height="83" /></a> Quest Complete</span></h3>
<p>Quest Complete - You have slain <a href="/wiki/Merveil" class="mw-redirect" title="Merveil">Merveil</a>. You are able to travel to <a href="/wiki/Act_2" title="Act 2">Act 2</a> now.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Quest_rewards">Quest rewards</span></h2>
<p>All of the quest rewards are rewarded to the player when reaching <a href="/wiki/The_Cavern_of_Wrath" title="The Cavern of Wrath">The Cavern of Wrath</a> and then talk to <a href="/wiki/Nessa" title="Nessa">Nessa</a> in <a href="/wiki/Lioneye%27s_Watch_(Act_1)" title="Lioneye&#39;s Watch (Act 1)">the town</a>, and does not need to kill <a href="/wiki/Merveil,_the_Siren" title="Merveil, the Siren">Merveil, the Siren</a>.
</p>
